National Production Conference Declaration (3)

Mining Industry

To further develop production, let's discuss the mining industry. Developing the mining industry to enhance rear area production and enrich national finances is a crucial task at present. The mineral resources of the southwest and northwest provinces related to national defense, military needs, or civil industries include coal, iron, oil, copper, and zinc in provinces such as Sichuan, Kang (Xikang), Shaanxi, Gansu, Zhejiang, Yunnan, and Guizhou. Those related to international trade or foreign exchange include gold, tin, tungsten, antimony, and mercury in provinces such as Kang (Xikang), Qinghai, Sichuan, Shaanxi, Henan, Hubei, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Guangxi. Their distribution is wide, and their reserves are abundant. Furthermore, new mines are constantly being discovered, demanding full development. In the future, the unexploited mineral resources in the southwest and northwest provinces should be actively explored, and the best ones should be selected for mining and smelting. For existing mines and smelters, regardless of whether they use modern or traditional methods, efforts should be intensified to promote guidance, maintenance, adjustment, expansion, and improvement to achieve the greatest possible effect with available funds in the near future. Regarding the expenses for exploring new mines or expanding, improving, and relocating smelters, if there are insufficient funds, the government should allocate funds to assist, so that both state-owned and private mines can develop simultaneously, ensuring that the resources for the War of Resistance and national reconstruction will not be depleted. For state-owned mines, emphasis should be placed on cooperation between the central and provincial governments. This is the first point.

Sales and Transportation Methods

Regarding the sales and transportation of mineral products, they can be classified based on type as either for export or for domestic consumption. For mineral products that maintain foreign exchange and develop international trade, constructing or improving international railways to facilitate exports is crucial. For mineral products that supply domestic industry and military needs, branch lines of domestic railways should be connected to major mining areas in advance to increase transportation capacity and reduce transportation costs, time, and effort, so that the production and smelting of various important mineral products can gradually meet the corresponding supply and demand. As for mineral products that should be under state control, the central government should manage them in a unified manner. Any special control measures originally established by the provinces should be abolished to achieve consistency. This is the second point.

Talent Cultivation

Regarding the cultivation of mining industry talent, domestic university mining and metallurgy departments should emphasize both theory and practice. In addition to mining and metallurgy, students should be assigned to major mines and smelters for practical training. For mineral processing, equipment should be increased to allow students to practice at any time to prepare for application, so that various mixed ore minerals can be fully distinguished, utilized, and increase efficiency. In addition, special attention should be paid to the training of mine foremen and workers. This is the third point.

Administrative Laws and Regulations

Regarding iron industry administration, based on the current situation of the domestic mining industry, it is gradually becoming more consistent than before. However, the responsible government agencies in various provinces should strive for unification and simplification, and urge the increase in mineral production. It is not only necessary to increase surveying teams to facilitate the people's access to mining rights, but also to strictly enforce mining laws. For mines that have already obtained permits but have not yet started construction or have suspended work, strict measures should be taken to avoid the virtual occupation of mining areas and hindering production. For mines where people have applied for mining rights but have not yet been surveyed, they should be urged to conduct surveys within a limited time and transfer the permits to facilitate merchants and benefit production. In addition to the temporary measures for limited application and management of coal and gold mines that the government has already promulgated, the expansions that were previously approved for mining by the responsible government agencies in various provinces should all be presented for replacement with permits, in order to consolidate mining rights. Old soil mines that are privately mined should be ordered to establish rights in accordance with the law within a limited time to avoid affecting the entire mining industry. This is the fourth point. The above four points are all matters that the central and local governments should urgently undertake for mining production, and should be implemented earnestly to benefit the mining administration. The development and construction of agriculture, forestry, industry, and mining have been outlined, but without complete and inexpensive transportation, even if production increases, sales will be hindered, which will not only fail to supplement military supplies but may also lead to blockage and collapse. Production relies on transportation to facilitate flow, and then supply and demand can be adjusted, and trade can prosper, leading to development and prosperity. Moreover, during the War of Resistance, the basic resources needed for national defense and the large quantities of products exported rely on transportation as their lifeline. The southwest and northwest regions are vast, with continuous mountains, and relying solely on highway transportation is not only too slow to be effective but also too wasteful. The newly built international transportation railways cannot be completed in a short period of time. If no other remedies are taken, the future will become increasingly difficult. Today, those who discuss economic construction in the southwest place too much emphasis on alleviating the current commercial suffering and neglect the study of transportation, resulting in the problem of mismatch between supply and demand. The current plan must be to adjust all transportation materials and统筹(coordinate) them, and adjust the quantity of various materials, transportation capacity, the amount of labor and materials, and the presence or absence of motive power before pushing the entire work of产运销存(production, transportation, sales, and storage). We believe that today's transportation construction, in addition to the international transportation lines in the southwest and northwest, should be considered. The key to saving time is: first, the construction of light railways. Although standard railways have their advantages, they are too expensive and take too long, which is not as fast as the completion of light railways. They are cheap and easy to popularize, so it is recommended that the government promptly prepare for the construction of light railways, which should be listed as the main body of land transportation tools; The second is the sorting out of the existing highways, such as the reduction of the gradient, the improvement of the roadbed, the strengthening of the bridges, and the addition of ferry boats, which are all important tasks for today's transportation improvement. The righteous or difficult to implement because of the cost of the project, and do not know that under the current deteriorating state of the highway, the damage of automobiles every year is calculated in hundreds of millions of yuan, which can sort out the national highway and have more than enough. The third is the application of human and animal power. After the highways are sorted out, the new improved carriages can pass unimpeded, using our country's own timber to build cars, using our own mules and horses to transport, not only cheap and labor-saving, and the foreign exchange burden due to gasoline saving will also be uncountable. Fourthly, the drainage of waterway, the southwest provinces, with vertical and horizontal canals, are rich in the profit of boats. A little drainage can be used for boats, and wood can be cut down the mountain to build ships along the river. The amount of a boat exceeds the car, which is not only convenient for military transportation, but also can smooth the flow of goods. The improvement of domestic transportation tools is more difficult to clumsy 塞到外的漏巵(leak of blocking) and increase the convenience of transportation. All four of these suggestions are easy to implement. If they can be promoted step by step, they can not only benefit military transportation, but also help the development of production and construction. (To be continued)

British New Note Sent to Moscow, Lloyd George and Others Deliver Passionate Speeches, France Hopes UK and Soviet Union Will Establish an Agreement Quickly

[Associated Press, Paris, 19th] According to senior diplomatic officials here, who told the Associated Press reporter last night, British Foreign Secretary Halifax has already notified the French government that Britain has accepted the Soviet Union's proposal in principle. If the Soviet Union provokes a war due to assistance to Poland, Romania, and Turkey, Britain will provide assistance on a reciprocal basis. They also notified the French government that Britain's new note is on its way to Moscow. In the note, Britain suggests that the UK, France, and the Soviet Union mutually guarantee each other to deal with wars caused by the UK and France due to assistance to Poland, Romania, and Turkey. However, Britain still refuses to guarantee the small Baltic countries, but may invite the Soviet Union to participate in a joint guarantee to Poland, Romania, and Turkey. If the Soviet Union provokes a war due to assistance to Poland, Romania, and Turkey, the UK and France will certainly provide assistance.

[Haitong News Agency, Paris, 18th] According to political figures here, Britain's new note was sent out this afternoon. The British note is based on the original French plan, stating that if the Soviet Union is drawn into the war due to assistance to countries guaranteed by Britain and France, Britain and France will provide assistance. In other words, if the Soviet Union gets into the war due to assisting Poland and Romania, Britain and France will immediately provide assistance.

[Haitong News Agency, Paris, 18th] Before the British reply to the Soviet Union was sent out, diplomatic negotiations were underway. Soviet Ambassador Maisky visited the British Foreign Office several times. After the visit, he returned to the embassy and discussed with Moscow by long-distance telephone. The press here, especially 'Le Radicale', hopes that the UK-Soviet agreement can be established in the near future and believes that Chamberlain will be able to present a concrete report at the House of Commons meeting tomorrow afternoon. According to the newspaper's opinion, Britain does not want to take on too much burden in the current situation, so it is unwilling to publicly establish a military agreement, so as not to give more basis to the theory of encircling the Axis countries. 'Le Radicale' also stated that France had urged Britain to establish an agreement with the Soviet Union as soon as possible. 'Le Parisien' denied that the Foreign Office had put forward a compromise plan and said that if there was still no success when the League of Nations met, Halifax might go to Moscow.

[Reuters, London, 19th] Lloyd George delivered a passionate speech in the House of Commons today in a debate on diplomatic events, referring to the next action of the dictatorial countries. He said, "The preparation of the dictatorial countries at this time is unprecedented and worthy of attention. Its purpose is to defeat us. If we want to obtain peace in place of alley warfare, we can only prepare military strength to deal with emergencies and cooperate with all countries to resist aggression. Regarding the Soviet Union, if we are unwilling to approach it, but we have made guarantees to Poland and Romania, why not quickly decide to conclude an agreement with the Soviet Union, just like establishing an agreement with France?" Opposition leader Attlee believed that Lloyd George had made a dark and true statement about the current world situation. Attlee believes that Britain has no constructive peace efforts at present, but is only waiting for the next act of aggression, and said, "We must recognize the aggressive policy of the Axis countries. The armed thugs in Europe are prepared to blackmail anyone."

Chamberlain Discusses Foreign Policy

[Reuters, London, 19th] When the House of Commons debated foreign policy today, Prime Minister Chamberlain (pictured) rose to speak after Attlee to cheers from the crowd. He began by saying that he did not want to discuss diplomatic issues today, because the present time is a tense, urgent, and apprehensive period. He knows very well that his words can be heard not only by all members, but also by the whole world, and studied carefully. "There are some people who have ulterior motives and specialize in picking on words, which may distort what is said today and produce misleading meanings. Mr. Attlee has said that a long-term peace policy is needed, and the colonial issue is also a part of it. We in this country have no intention of buying peace at the price of concessions, so it is enough to cause endless demands. However, this does not mean that we refuse to discuss with other countries any way to satisfy the emotions of other countries, even if that method is to revise the current situation. We are also willing to discuss it. If this method can guarantee a discussion in a good atmosphere, the problem may be easily solved. If there are no special difficulties during the negotiation, there may be more concessions, but the acquisition of this concession must be used for what it has promised, and cannot infringe upon the freedom of others. Until we are completely satisfied that the other party has abandoned the attempt to invade others, it is difficult for us to discuss the final conditions of peace.

German Government's Actions Contradict Guarantees

The German government has declared that it has no intention of annexing others, but unfortunately, those who oppose it dare not believe it, and there are many. This attitude of disbelief is also what the German government has caused (cheers). If we are sure that the other party has abandoned the attempt to invade and has no intention of using force between Germany and other countries, I believe that we will not shrink back for long and explain our views and routes for discussing permanent peace. The United States' greatest desire is to maintain peace, which should be believed with an international spirit. Britain's desire is only that various needs can be balanced in order to achieve the best completion. This means that the requirements and rights of all countries should be taken into account, and then we can discuss how to establish a route for lasting peace." Referring to Lloyd George's speech, Chamberlain said that he did not ignore the seriousness of the situation, but Lloyd George exaggerated it. There is nothing unusual or surprising about the withdrawal of the British Embassy in Prague. Regarding the permission to transfer Czech property abroad, which is helpful to Germany, Chamberlain said, "I really don't know whether the German government knows that its actions have caused a major reaction around the world. I believe that the German government's actions completely contradict the guarantees it has repeatedly given to the world. It has caused more unease among people around the world than its annexation of others. This contradiction has completely destroyed the sense of security and created a widespread feeling that once any small country is noticed by Germany's ambitions, it will be difficult to preserve its independence. Therefore, we increasingly feel that if we cannot use some new elements to stabilize the situation today, a large part of the European continent will disintegrate. The British government, in view of this, feels that it should immediately join hands with France to intervene. If France provides the above-mentioned elements to stabilize the situation, the threat of German aggression is quite acute, so we have to persuade quickly. However, the guarantees we have made to Poland and Turkey are not the final goal of our plan. These guarantees are proposed to avoid further deterioration of the situation, and can be called 'emergency measures'. In other words, we should go further and plan for a more permanent countermeasure to strengthen the power of the above guarantee and try to reach out to other great powers who are willing to contribute assistance. Although, I would still like to be clear that our policy does not mean that the European countries will form hostile groups. The formation of these groups is incited by mutual 'bad feelings' and they think the war is inevitable. Before the war has broken out, I never feel that war is inevitable, and the dimmer the situation and the more pressing the war is, the more I feel the need to make efforts to stop the war. We believe that any policy, if it aims to create hostile groups, is inherently unstable, so it is fundamentally dangerous. As for the policy we are following today, it has no aggressive components, and we will never refuse the opportunity to discuss all differences with an international spirit of amity. This is a policy of precaution and will not be implemented unless in a certain situation.

Must Prevent Violent Aggression

Whether that certain situation will happen or not, the power is in the hands of other countries. This means that our policy is to prevent violent acts of aggression. Acts of aggression may not happen, and we hope that they will never happen. This is a necessary policy. Without this policy, we cannot achieve stability in Europe, and the lives of businesses will be affected, and the living conditions of the people cannot be improved. We have offered guarantees to several countries, but this is not enough. We are willing to have other countries join and assist these countries together, so we are negotiating with the Soviet Union and Turkey. Regarding the UK-Turkish negotiations, the UK and Turkish governments quickly expressed the same interests and opinions, so a declaration was established on May 12. The declaration was warmly welcomed, which is enough to show the honor of Turkey and the preciousness of its friendship. UK-Turkish friendship began during the era of President Kemal, and under the current President, this friendship is increasing day by day.

The South Agrees in Principle to Join the German-Italian Axis: Agreements of Non-Aggression to be Signed with Germany, Italy, and Hungary; German-Estonian Talks Near Completion

[Reuters, London, 19th] The "News Chronicle's" correspondent in the Yugoslavian capital reports that Prince Paul has returned from Rome. His discussions with Italian Foreign Minister Ciano have resulted in a preliminary agreement for Yugoslavia to join the German-Italian Axis. The practical implementation of this decision will involve Yugoslavia separately concluding non-aggression pacts with Germany, Italy, and Hungary (i.e., a three-way non-aggression pact between Southern Germany, Southern Italy, and Southern Hungary). The specific details will be determined by Ciano and Ribbentrop in Berlin. Yugoslav officials believe this is a sound move, arguing that the Anglo-Turkish agreement has rendered the Balkan Entente obsolete.

[Reuters, Berlin, 18th] Regarding negotiations between Germany and the Baltic and Scandinavian countries, a communiqué has been issued stating that German talks with Estonia and Latvia are nearing completion. An agreement in principle has also been reached with Denmark to establish a non-aggression pact soon. However, the governments of Sweden, Norway, and Finland have declared that they do not feel threatened by Germany and, therefore, see no need to enter into non-aggression agreements with Germany.

[Reuters, Rome, 18th] Italy and Romania have concluded a commodity exchange agreement. Italy will exchange rayon, textiles, automobiles, and machinery for 80,000 tons of grain and 350,000 tons of kerosene from Romania. Italy has also agreed to assist Romania in developing its maritime transport industry.

Spain Officially Declares the End of the Civil War: Franco Participates in Victory Parade in Madrid

[Reuters, Burgos, 18th] Celebrations of victory began today in various locations in Spain, continuing for two days, to formally declare the end of the Civil War. General Franco will participate in a victory parade in Madrid tomorrow, with an army of 100,000 soldiers.

Brief Commentary

Abrupt Tensions in the Shanghai International Settlement

According to news reports today, the situation in the Shanghai International Settlement has suddenly become tense. Settlement authorities have implemented special martial law, with all foreign troops, police, and volunteer corps mobilized. The streets and alleys are filled with uniforms, firearms, and barbed wire, creating a state of wartime readiness.

The fundamental reason for the tension in Shanghai lies in Japan's preparation to implement armed occupation. The sudden and unprecedented surge in tension in the past two days indicates that the settlement authorities are unwilling to surrender all rights and interests to Japan. The emergency measures taken by the settlement authorities, similar to the landing of British, American, and French sailors on Gulangyu, is a clear warning to Japan: "Do not go too far. Britain, America, and France will not easily withdraw from the Far East!"

However, we remain pessimistic about the future of Shanghai, as we do about the Gulangyu incident and the situations in Tianjin and Hankou. Firstly, the desire to seize the concessions in Shanghai, Hankou, Tianjin, and other European powers' bases of influence and interests in the Far East is not only part of Japan's overall invasion plan, but also a necessary and urgent measure to remedy and reverse their setbacks in the invasion of China. Therefore, unless subjected to effective strikes by European and American powers, Japan's harassing actions will never "stop at the appropriate point"! All menacing threats are simply Japan's proud tactics and will certainly not scare them away! Secondly, the measures currently taken by the European and American democratic and peaceful countries to restrain Japan are obviously not strong enough. Moreover, the tactics employed by the settlement authorities today, such as overstepping their authority to suppress Chinese newspapers that support China, and carrying out large-scale crackdowns on anti-Japanese elements, may be said to be aimed at avoiding pretexts for Japan to provoke greater incidents. However, since Japan is looking for opportunities, they will not lack excuses. Instead of upholding law and order based on justice and the concession bylaws, they are yielding to Japan's demands by violating the laws, which not only undermine their own position but also provide Japan with opportunities to exploit. In the future, all Chinese residents in the concessions can be labeled as anti-Japanese or communist, and even if all Chinese are expelled, Westerners can still be accused of supporting China, being anti-Japanese, or being communist. What unimaginable disasters will lie ahead?

Therefore, we believe that in order to prevent Japan from further implementing armed occupation and annexation, the landing of British, American, and French sailors on Gulangyu and the adoption of wartime preparations by the Shanghai settlement authorities as demonstrations of strength against Japan are absolutely necessary and appropriate. We believe that our compatriots residing in Shanghai and other concessions will be happy to accept various restrictions in order to see the demonstrations of strength by democratic and peaceful allies such as Britain, America, and France. However, if there are only these demonstrations without further effective restraints on Japan, or even if these demonstrations severely suppress all anti-Japanese and anti-aggression forces, it will not only fail to prevent Japan's further encroachments but may even fuel their arrogance! Therefore, our task today is to intensify all diplomatic efforts, urge democratic and peaceful countries such as Britain, America, and France not to miss the last opportunity, strengthen their own unity, and step up efforts to support China and restrain Japan. Otherwise, what China loses will be only this much, while the European and American democratic and peaceful allies will be forced to withdraw completely from the Far East. In addition, all parties should learn from the experiences of Shanghai and Gulangyu, become serious and vigilant, abandon decadent and degenerate behaviors, and actively promote all work to return to the country and assist the motherland! Times are critical, don't dream anymore!

Local News

Air Defense Commissioner Officially Announces Emergency Air Defense Drills Will Be Conducted at Any Time: No Prior Notice Will Be Given to Residents, Who Should Be Prepared for Blackouts at All Times; Seven New Siren Machines Arriving from England Will Reach Hong Kong During the Day

Hong Kong's air defense work, according to the original plan of the Hong Kong government, is being actively carried out. After more than ten months, considerable progress has been made, and the air defense work has entered another stage. It is understood that the current air defense authorities are actively seeking residents' cooperation with the government, widely promoting air defense, so that all residents of Hong Kong, regardless of gender or age, can understand and acquire knowledge about escaping air raids. On the one hand, they are intensifying the planning of disaster relief locations and the deployment of resident evacuation, so that in the event of war and Hong Kong being attacked, residents can follow the common sense they have acquired and evacuate in an orderly manner, without being caught off guard. Regarding blackout drills, several have been held in the past two years, but they have all been of a general nature. The authorities announced the dates in advance each time. This kind of regular exercise cannot meet the needs of wartime. Therefore, the Air Defense Committee has decided to hold a wartime air defense exercise in the near future to train residents to respond to emergencies. Regarding the duration of the exercise, the authorities have not yet made a clear announcement. The reporter interviewed the Air Defense Commissioner yesterday, who said that the air defense exercise could be held at any time. In order to test whether residents can calmly cope, the date must be kept secret and no prior notice will be given. During this period, residents of Hong Kong should be fully prepared at all times to avoid panic in an emergency. As for the sirens, the number was previously too small, and the sirens could not be spread to all areas of Hong Kong. Since the new sirens arrived from England a few days ago, a test has been done and good results have been obtained. A total of six of these new sirens have now arrived in Hong Kong, distributed in various areas of Hong Kong. There are still seven more being shipped from England and will arrive in Hong Kong during the day. The installation locations of these seven new sirens have not yet been determined and may be distributed in the Kowloon area in the future.

China Salvation Drama Troupe Hosts Reception Today: Benefit Performances are Imminent, Departing Abroad Immediately After Performances to Seek Guidance; Notable Figures from All Walks of Life Invited to Attend

The China Salvation Drama Troupe, which has been fighting on the northern front for twenty months and is loved by millions of soldiers and civilians, will go to the Nanyang area to comfort overseas Chinese and complete a greater propaganda and economic mission. Increasing Water Supply in Hong Kong: Submarine Water Pipes Near Completion; Can Temporarily Increase Water Supply by One Million Gallons; Will Increase to Sixteen Million Gallons in the Future

In order to increase the amount of water supplied to Hong Kong, the Hong Kong Water Authority has added a submarine water pipe to transport water stored in the Shing Mun Reservoir to Hong Kong. The project began in November last year and has been underway for several months. The completion date is not far away. The last few sections of the water pipes were also installed in the sea in front of the Queen's Pier yesterday. After the new pipe is installed, the amount of water supplied to Hong Kong Island from the Shing Mun Reservoir will increase compared to before. The old pipe supplied 8 million gallons of water per day to Hong Kong Island from the Shing Mun Reservoir. The new pipe will temporarily increase the supply by 1 million gallons. Once the second new main pipe is installed in the Kowloon Peninsula, it can be increased to 16 million gallons. The new main pipe has now been installed to Waterloo Road, where the water source will be connected. The Public Works Department engineers encountered many difficulties during the installation of the new submarine water pipe. When it was placed in the middle of Hong Kong Harbour, the project was suspended from time to time due to the rapid currents. Work could only be carried out when the flow slowed down. However, the difficulty of this project lies in connecting each section of the water pipe, ensuring that the two ends fit together perfectly. For this reason, the engineers used an installation machine for accurate measurement. This makes it easier for the coppersmiths to work. The inside diameter of the water pipe is 21 inches, and the old ones are only 12 or 18 inches. The inside of the pipe is attached with a layer of cement concrete, half an inch thick, to prevent corrosion. The outside is also attached with two and a half inches of cement concrete to prevent corrosion and damage from seawater and other causes. Each section of the water pipe is 55 feet long, and each two sections are connected with an extensible joint. After each section is connected, it is tested with a pressure of 300 pounds to see if it is properly connected. In addition, the project still has to connect to the Queen's Pier and the Kowloon Station underground. Once the work is completed in these two locations, the water supply to Hong Kong from the Kowloon Reservoir will be very abundant.

Special Feature of this Newspaper

Continue to Carry Forward the Fighting Spirit of the Martyrs: "Huanghuagang" to be Restaged Tonight: Hong Kong Film and Theater Circles Celebrate Mr. Ouyang Yuqian's Fiftieth Birthday

— Qi Zhuo

The spirit of "Huanghuagang" that created the Republic of China should be carried forward; the sensational Hong Kong performance of "Huanghuagang" should be repeated—

Time: Today and tomorrow;

Address: Kowloon Po Hing Theatre.

Why restage "Huanghuagang"?

First, to promote the spirit of fighting and sacrificing for national liberation;

Second, to raise funds for the Disaster Relief Federation to comfort the war dead and their families, and to comfort the martyrs in the afterlife;

Third, to consolidate and promote the unprecedented unity of the Hong Kong drama community.

In addition to the three points similar to the last time, there are new meanings in this restaging of "Huanghuagang".

First, the last performance of "Huanghuagang" was successful, and this great harvest should be broadcast;

Second, move to Kowloon in order to be universal. Let revolutionary thoughts and revolutionary actions occur in every corner.

Third, it is a gift from the Hong Kong drama community to celebrate the 50th birthday of Mr. Ouyang Yuqian, a drama instructor.

——Looking at it this way, this performance. The significance of "Huanghuagang" is even more profound than last time.

Why should Mr. Ouyang Yuqian's birthday be celebrated? Because Mr. Ouyang is a pioneer in the Chinese drama world, and his decades of fighting spirit are worthy of praise and pride. Since the Anti-Japanese War, he has made no small contribution to the salvation drama and national defense films. We should give this old and strong artistic pioneer comfort and encouragement.

In addition to the sincere birthday wishes and unlimited hopes from the drama community for Mr. Ouyang, the China Art Troupe specially held a banquet to celebrate last night. Invite cultural, film, and drama circles in Hong Kong, with more than 200 participants, and the atmosphere was warm and lively for a while. China Film Studio also sent staff to shoot news films, and it was not until 1:00 a.m. that the party ended. Tonight at 8:00 p.m., a joint benefit performance of "Huanghuagang" will be held at the Po Hing Theatre to celebrate. Tickets are priced at two dimes, five dimes, one yuan, and two yuan to make it universal. Singing groups attending include the Chinese Amateur Chorus, the Guofeng Hao Singing Team, the Chinese Bookstore Singing Team, and the Fourth Women's Training Class Singing Team. It is hoped that the compatriots in Hong Kong and Kowloon will not miss this rare opportunity. At the same time, the Central Theatre is screening "Xiao Lingzi", the Cathay Theatre is screening "The Peach Blossom Fan", and the Nathan Theatre is screening "Mulan Joins the Army" and other famous films to help celebrate. All income will be donated by Mr. Ouyang to the Disaster Relief Federations. The above films are all masterpieces of Mr. Ouyang, and the film rental is donated by Huacheng and Huasheng Companies, and the theatre rental is donated by Central, Cathay, and Nathan Theatres. This is also a first in Hong Kong.

——Such a birthday celebration is a unique expression of the film and drama circles and is a very meaningful event. Taking advantage of Mr. Ouyang's birthday today, in addition to paying our highest national tribute to Mr. Ouyang and wishing him eternal youth, we should provide some suggestions from the standpoint of a journalist as a birthday gift:

1. The united front and common development of the drama community is an urgent task at present. Even if some people do not have common beliefs or mutual trust, this is an inevitable transitional phenomenon. It is hoped that Mr. Ouyang will continue to work hard and lead it well.

2. It is hoped that under the leadership of Mr. Ouyang, "Chinese Art" will carry out more meaningful and other salvation work in addition to salvation dramas, which will surely have greater success and greater effect. "Even eating and love are related to the invasion of the enemy." Mr. Lu Xun's statement is not wrong in our common experience.

3. The members of the Chinese Art Troupe, who have been trained for many years, are quite skilled in acting. It is hoped that Mr. Ouyang will lead them to go further and shoulder greater tasks of the times in all aspects more substantively and strongly.

Landlords are Again Forcing Tenants to Install Water Meters Themselves: Using Water Meters as a Means to Exploit Housing and Increase Rent

Some landlords in Hong Kong, fearing the extension of the anti-eviction ordinance, are again carrying out last year's failed attempt. Before the Hong Kong government implemented the ice fee regulations on January 1st of this year, landlords took the opportunity to force tenants to install their own water meters under the pretext of complying with government regulations. Later, the authorities learned about this and promulgated an emergency ordinance, stating that if tenants were forced by landlords and not of their own free will, the Water Authority would reject their request. After the ordinance was implemented, the landlords had to comply. Recently, the landlords have not given up on this matter and have even consulted several times. The initial method is to ask the government to remove the existing water meters, and automatically reduce the rent, so that the tenants can install the water meters themselves and pay the water bills. The main purpose of the landlords is to earn an extra ten yuan in rent per water meter per year, and at the same time, they can get the deposit back. Secondly, there is a current shortage of housing. If the method is implemented, tenants will have to install their own water meters at a cost of sixty yuan (including the deposit, labor, and materials). Once installed, it will be difficult to move. At that time, the water meter can be used to exploit the tenants. If the tenant does not want to dismantle the meter when moving out and suffer losses, the landlord can take advantage of the situation and ask the tenant to find a replacement, and then rent it to a new tenant with high-sounding reasons and increase the rent again. Based on the above two points, it is no wonder that the landlords, who value money as their lives, disregard the suffering of the residents and act recklessly.

Guangdong Relief Association and Hong Kong and Macau Student Relief Committee: Teacher Registration Lottery Held Yesterday: More Than 300 People Were Hired as a Result

The Provincial Relief Association and the Hong Kong and Macau Student Relief Committee recently held teacher registration, which ended on the 14th. Statistics show that a total of 1,520 teachers registered in Hong Kong, Kowloon, and Macau. However, the quota was only 300. Therefore, the lottery was held at 2:00 p.m. yesterday at the library of the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce. Mr. Yi Boyang, the person in charge of the Relief Association, announced the reasons for the lottery, saying that there are currently 1,520 teachers registered in Hong Kong, Kowloon, and Macau. The Association has specially set the priority employment standards, and the employment methods are divided into six types: (1) Education: (1) Graduates of domestic and foreign university education departments, normal universities, or university normal departments or higher normal schools, (2) Graduates of old-style normal schools or new-style high school normal schools, (2) Experience: Served in a registered complete primary school for more than three years, (3) Teaching performance: Awarded by provincial, municipal, and county education departments or bureaus, (4) Certificates: Original certificates are fully submitted for inspection, (5) Family situation: Truly unemployed and the family is poor, (6) Service situation: Worked hard during the Anti-Japanese War. If each teacher has the above six conditions, he/she can get priority employment. Mr. Tan then said that the Association had recently selected 87 unemployed primary school teachers for priority recruitment, including 29 in Hong Kong, 37 in Kowloon, and 21 in Macau. However, there are the following four regulations for teachers who are given priority: (1) The teachers who are given priority will also be decided by lottery according to the standards set by the review committee, (2) The teachers to be employed in the future, except for those who are given priority, will be employed in order of lottery, (3) The teachers who are given priority or decided by lottery will receive a living allowance from the time they are officially appointed as teachers in the Association's charity school, (4) If a teacher who is given priority or obtained by lottery is found to have a job, he/she should be replaced in order. According to the results of the lottery yesterday, 159 people were hired. There were more than 300 people who were given priority and hired by lottery, of which 50 were alternates, with 35 in Hong Kong and Kowloon and 45 in Macau.

Li Huifang, the owner of a fishing boat, returned to Hong Kong from overseas the other day and told reporters about the experience of being robbed by an enemy ship. Around 8:00 a.m. on the 15th of this month, when his fishing boat was sailing in the waters of Sanmen, Huizhou, he suddenly saw two enemy ships towing six fishing boats, coming towards him. He thought that even if he tried to escape, he would still be caught by the enemy ship, so he continued to sail along the original route. When the two sides were close, the enemy ship ordered him to stop, and sent several enemy soldiers over to the ship to search. They robbed him of eight yuan and a cat before letting him go. Before leaving, they asked him to transport 32 of the fishermen who had been robbed back to Hong Kong, and then sailed away. According to the robbed fishermen, they were fishermen from six fishing boats. Within an hour, they were robbed by the enemy ship. There were hundreds of men and women on the ship. In addition to the 32 people who were fortunately released, the fate of the others is unknown.

Nanhua Singing Class

The quantity of goods stored in warehouses and stockpiles by the 20th of this month must be listed and reported to the county chamber of commerce for filing with this office. 2. If the quantity of goods exceeds the prescribed amount, except for one-third to be retained for market supply, the relocation must commence immediately and be completed by the end of May. Those who fail to relocate by the deadline will be investigated and confiscated according to the order. 3. The relocation location is to be chosen by the owners of the goods without restriction, but only inland relocation is permitted. 4. When relocating, the location and quantity must be reported by the guilds to the county chamber of commerce for filing and the county chamber of commerce must notify this office of the progress of the relocation by the 28th of this month for onward reporting. 5. Small merchants and peddlers may handle the relocation of goods at their discretion, but all goods must still be relocated when necessary. 6. New purchases of imported goods and industrial raw materials, in addition to the amount retained for market supply, should be transported inland and not stockpiled in the county seat.

(Xingning Correspondence) The Ministry of Finance has specially issued three measures for adjusting local finances in war zones and has consulted and sent them to Guangdong. The Department of Finance has immediately distributed the measures to all counties and cities under its jurisdiction for uniform implementation. The measures are as follows: 1. In guerrilla areas, all tax deductions should be announced and abolished, and the people in the area should be persuaded to refuse to pay taxes to any party. 2. In areas that are currently in combat, whether or not to start, appease, or reduce/exempt various taxes shall be decided by the provincial authorities in charge according to the conditions in each area, and shall be executed by the financial institutions in the respective areas. The methods and locations of collection shall be designed to provide full convenience to the people, and the army is strictly prohibited from directly collecting and apportioning taxes from the people or illegally requisitioning. 3. In areas close to the war, all legal local taxes should still be collected as usual, but miscellaneous taxes must be completely abolished, and illegal apportionment and requisitioning are strictly prohibited.

"Dead City" Four-Day Experience Record

A representative of the Hong Kong South China Morning Post recently traveled from Hong Kong to Guangzhou and stayed in the "Dead City" for four days. Upon his return, he wrote a "Dead City" Four-Day Experience Record, which was published in the newspaper. It provides a factual report on the desolate state of Guangzhou under _____ occupation, the chaotic financial situation, and the dark world of rampant robbers. The absurdity of the _____ propaganda that Guangzhou has recovered its prosperity can be refuted by anyone who has been to Guangzhou, and the _____ plot to attract people back to the city is difficult to achieve. The true face of Guangzhou after the fall can be glimpsed by reading the article.

The article first describes the author's experience of arriving in Guangzhou from Macau and the impressions he gained. He said that upon arriving in Guangzhou, on the way from the dock to Shamian by rickshaw, he was able to glimpse the face of Guangzhou after the looting. The first impression was reminiscent of the reports of the Great Fire of Guangzhou in the newspapers. The dilapidated walls and desolate scenery. Few large buildings were spared by the fire. The embankment was relatively prosperous. Most of the streets were deserted. Public buses and private cars were rare. The only vehicles running on the road were Japanese military vehicles, shuttling back and forth busily. At street intersections, there were often many Japanese soldiers, searching pedestrians in groups. Every few hundred yards, there was a Japanese soldier on sentry duty, with a stern look, making passers-by avoid him. Shamian was also affected, with business being unusually sluggish. Although the stores were open as usual, the staff had been greatly reduced. The Victoria Hotel was deserted, with only the author and his companion as guests. The number of foreigners in Shamian had sharply decreased, from several hundred to only fifty. Prices were the same as in Hong Kong, but fruits and vegetables were surprisingly expensive. Imported goods were no longer available in Guangzhou, and the shops sold Japanese goods. Most of the shops in the city were run by Japanese. Guangzhou has become a dumping ground for Japanese goods.

The financial situation in Guangzhou is extremely chaotic. The Japanese army ordered the citizens to use Japanese military scrip and prohibited the circulation of legal tender. However, most citizens were happy to use legal tender, so legal tender was still circulating in the market, but stores and restaurants run by the Japanese refused to use it. Guangzhou has become a dead city, with desolation everywhere. Few citizens have returned to the city. The exact number of people in Guangzhou is difficult to ascertain. According to a merchant in Shamian, it is estimated to be about 500,000, but another estimate is 150,000. According to a Japanese merchant, it is said that it is no more than 200,000 at most. According to the author's observation, the current population of Guangzhou is about 100,000, mostly from the poor classes. Although some merchants once returned to the city, they soon reopened because the area was unstable, robbers were rampant, and there was no business to be done. Those who were slightly wealthy were unwilling to stay in the dead city to be disturbed. Because the city was unstable, a curfew was announced at night. In fact, the Japanese army was on high alert day and night. There are about 10,000 Japanese soldiers in the city. As for whether or not there were battles taking place in the suburbs, it was difficult to ascertain. According to a Japanese military officer who spoke to the author, there were no battles within 30 miles of Guangzhou, but two days ago, Shamian still heard clear artillery fire. While the author was staying in Guangzhou, he often saw Japanese military vehicles carrying large numbers of wounded Japanese soldiers back to the city.

Movies and Drama

Charlie Chaplin Receives Threats While Filming His New Film "The Dictator". Employs Special Guards for Rotation. Decides Not to Waver from His Original Intention and Works Hard to Proceed.

Charlie Chaplin, the giant of screen comedy, is making his new sound film, "The Dictator," the content of which, as everyone knows, is a satire of a certain dictator. He emphasizes the stupidity and absurdity of certain barbaric and unreasonable political phenomena in the current world situation and brings them to the screen in the form of comedy.

Striking the soul of those people before the world, of course, will make a certain kind of person feel angry and threatened, and therefore use their consistent rogue methods against Chaplin—threats—murder.

"The Dictator" has already started filming and is currently being actively produced. However, since it was decided to film this film, Chaplin has received countless threatening letters, mostly saying that "The Dictator" contains "defamatory" meanings, and demanding that he stop filming immediately, otherwise they will use terrorist methods to "put Chaplin to death." In order to prevent being murdered, Chaplin has recently hired an armed bodyguard who stays close to him to protect him day and night. Special detectives are also sent to monitor him while he eats his three meals a day to prevent bad people from poisoning him. At the same time, during the filming of the film, the surroundings of the studio are also guarded, and the situation is quite serious. However, it is said that although Chaplin has been threatened by the terrorists, his original intention has not wavered in the slightest. On the contrary, the production of "The Dictator" is currently being actively intensified, day and night, in order to present "this ridiculous comedy to the world's forward-thinking people" in the shortest possible time. According to Hollywood filmmakers, it is unprecedented in film history to be so heavily guarded, as if they were important figures in the political world.

Movie Novel

Pygmalion (4) Produced by MGM. Original work by George Bernard Shaw. Starring Leslie Howard and Wendy Hiller.

"I said I would make her like a duchess." As he said that, he excitedly took out a large envelope, "Look, this is an invitation to a dance from the Transylvanian Embassy. I have decided to take her there as a duchess."

The day to leave for the dance was getting closer and closer. Eliza worked hard to learn all the manners and etiquette, and finally that day came quickly. Higgins scratched his messy hair and said to Eliza, "Let's practice one more time."

She was extremely tired, covered her face with her hands, and said disappointedly, "I—I can't do it."

Although there were many things in the embassy's magnificent ballroom that were worth being interested in, Higgins stood absentmindedly next to Pickering, because he was uneasily stepping onto the key to success and failure, worried about the outcome. He had just seen a face that dispelled his hopes. This man now walked over, a smile on his face, and said,

"Professor Higgins, do you remember me? I am Alex Carbotti. You taught me phonetics. You can point out where a person was born in England, but I can point out where they were born in Europe. I am your best student."

Higgins knew that the man indeed had the same ability as himself. After the man left, he told Pickering, "If he hears Eliza, I'm done."

"I want a better job," he continued. "But because my accent is wrong, people don't want me. Can you help me?"

South China Football Team to Play Charity Match with Joint Team Today. Hui Tang of South China and Da Gao of Joint Team to Compete. South China to Play Friendly Match with Foreign Sailors Tomorrow.

(Special report from this newspaper) The South China Athletic Association's football team, in the 1928-29 season, established a glorious achievement that will benefit future generations. It is truly rare and will be forever immortalized.

However, although their players have the glory of winning championships, they still do not consider this to be satisfactory. For learning is endless, and diligence leads to success. Recently, in response to an invitation from the Nanyang region, they are making an expedition again, departing on the 24th of this month on the French postal ship Bodume.

Even on the eve of departure, they are still generous. The South China touring team, at the invitation of the association's emergency work service corps, will play a charity match with the joint team at Caroline Hill at 5:15 pm today. This move is both for the sake of the compatriots in distress and also an opportunity to practice fully in preparation for the tour of Southeast Asia.

Today's tickets are divided into three types: one dollar, sixty cents, and thirty cents. However, viewers must not buy them outside the stadium, because fake tickets have recently appeared. Please do not be fooled.

Tomorrow at 5:15 pm, the touring team has also arranged a friendly match with the sailors of the British warship HMS Gannet, also at Caroline Hill. The ticket prices may be cheaper than today.

After the football season ends, many players go into seclusion. Therefore, although today's lineup for the joint team is arranged by the association, the South China Athletic Association first sought the consent of each member, who all agreed to contribute to the charity. This is how it can be realized. Since they have agreed to play, it is believed that they will not back down at the last minute.

The lineup for the joint team was announced the day before yesterday and looks exceptionally complete. The forward line has Da Gao, Shan Nu, Hou Chengtuo, Tuo Ban, etc., all first-class players, and their attacking power will definitely be sharp. The defense has Gu Ba, Xu Jingcheng, Hou Rongheng, Shi Han, etc., who are also well-known figures. If they all work together, it will definitely be pleasing to the eye.

The lineup for South China was only decided yesterday afternoon, showing a completely new look. In particular, the forward line has been positioned to suit each individual's abilities, and there is no longer the disadvantage of forcing people into positions they are not suited for. Moreover, in addition to the two wings being fixed, the three forwards can mutually adjust their positions when necessary, because all three forwards are suitable for both left and right, and can perform as desired in any position. This is the characteristic of today's forward line.

Some people say, "In exhibition matches that have no championship implications, the performances are never very intense." This situation may exist, but it is not necessarily the case. Because the two teams become enemies when they face each other. All who are involved in the battle will undoubtedly have the mentality of doing their best and striving for victory. Especially when the teams are evenly matched, the competition is even fiercer. They will not abandon their goal of achieving victory simply because there is no championship involved. It is believed that today these two teams, precisely because they are evenly matched, will have the ambition to not give in easily and will have the most exciting performances. Forging Football Tickets Defendant Guilty Fined or Imprisoned

Xu Ruifen, a teenager, 18 years old, was charged with selling four forged South China Athletic Association tickets at Caroline Hill on the 17th of this month. The case was heard yesterday morning by the Central Patrol Court. The case was prosecuted by English detective Jia Shiman. It was stated that the final battle for the Xuhe Cup was held at the South China Stadium at 5:15 pm on the 17th of this month. At that time, many people from all walks of life bought tickets to enter the stadium. At that time, the defendant was holding four South China Athletic Association fifty-cent tickets and selling them to people. He charged sixty cents for each ticket. Later, a person named Ou Yaoliang, without realizing it, bought the ticket from the defendant. When he held the ticket to enter the stadium, the gatekeeper discovered that it was a fake ticket. The official asked the defendant where he printed this kind of fake ticket. The defendant said that this kind of fake ticket was printed at a printing office at a certain number on Luoke Road. English detective Jia Shiman then stated to the official that when the police obtained the defendant's confession, they had already sent personnel to investigate the printing office, but the office did not have this kind of fake ticket. The official sentenced the defendant to a fine of fifty yuan or two months in prison.

Current Students' Reforms for Physical Training Should Have (3)

— Zou Falu

Gymnastics has always been criticized as being rigid and boring, and the amount of exercise is minimal. Students who only value freedom will not even bother to look at it. However, it has special value: the difficulty is profound, the boundaries are clear, and the old, young, strong, and weak can all do it; it is symmetrical on the left and right, and comprehensive on the top and bottom, and all parts of the body can benefit; it does not choose time and place, and does not limit the number of people, and can be done anytime and anywhere; and its main feature is that it does not require a small amount of money, and it is the basic exercise of all sports.

Activated apparatus gymnastics is an exercise that most people think is too difficult to do, but movements such as vaulting over the pommel horse and side horse and releasing the hand on the uneven bars can foster a spirit of boldness, carefulness, bravery, and adventure; exercises on the mat, such as handstands, single and double swings, rotations, etc., can cultivate a sense of response to obvious rotations and rapid ascents and descents in aviation technology; and the dexterity and agility of the movements can also cultivate the ability to cope with ease when fighting on the battlefield.

Guoshu (Chinese martial arts) is a traditional method of body training in our country for thousands of years. The subtlety of its movements and the mystery of its changes are its unique functions. Although modern warfare relies on airplanes and cannons, when it comes to charging and hand-to-hand combat, Guoshu can show great power. In the past war of resistance, there were countless glorious battles in which the power of Guoshu was used to kill enemies.

Military sports, such as climbing, crossing obstacles, jumping over obstacles, climbing mountains, rolling forward, and throwing hand grenades, not only can be directly applied in the event of a battle, achieving the effect of being able to handle things with ease, command freely, and kill enemies; but also is a sport that is rich in naturalness, and we can use it as a substitute for track and field.

Although the above-mentioned sports have not been completely covered, they have given an outline. We can choose and follow them according to the current needs of sports rehabilitation, and considering the performance of various sports. Students can also understand the reforms needed for physical training materials.

3. Reform of practice methods: Exercise can strengthen the body, and whether the effect can be achieved quickly depends on whether the practice method is appropriate. If the practice method is appropriate, there is no need to be timid and look around, and the work done will not be in vain at all; otherwise, hesitating and hesitating will inevitably lead to futile efforts.

Economic Column

Shanghai Lacks Investment Opportunities; Changes in the Domestic Economic Environment; The Abnormal Prosperity of the Shanghai Market Should Not Be Overly Optimistic; Development of the Southwest Economy Depends on Transportation Construction; Annual Report of Rising Banks

The annual report of the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank for the 27th year of the Republic [1938] stated: Due to the spread of war, the domestic economic situation this year has suffered unprecedented misfortune, and the losses have been the heaviest in our country's history. Moreover, due to the different impacts of the war on various regions, various abnormal phenomena have occurred. In general, both production and consumption have declined. As for the economic situation abroad, the situations in various countries vary greatly due to different environments and policies, but signs of recession seem to be more prevalent. The following is a summary of the domestic economic situation, divided into finance, trade, prices, and industry and commerce:

Finance: Following the financial panic of last autumn, the "Regulations for Stabilizing Finance" promulgated by the Ministry of Finance continued to be implemented. The Discount and Loan Committee organized by the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Farmers Bank of China also successively handled discount and loan matters in various regions. In addition, the government was determined to maintain the legal tender, and the governments and financial institutions of friendly countries such as the United Kingdom and the United States also provided assistance when appropriate. Therefore, although the war situation deteriorated day by day, the financial market was able to remain stable as usual. Not only was there no run on banks, but a large amount of previously fled capital also returned. Except for a few small banks, no financial institutions went bankrupt. The Shanghai interbank lending rate did not fluctuate abnormally throughout the year, and even the unofficial market for government bonds rose steadily. All of this was beyond our expectations and is gratifying. In this relatively stable situation, there were also some important events that deserve our attention, roughly as follows:

Black Market for Foreign Exchange: At the beginning of this year, the government continued to strive to maintain the statutory exchange rate. Later, due to environmental factors, on March 14, the "Measures for Foreign Exchange Application and Verification" were promulgated, stipulating that when banks needed foreign exchange for legitimate purposes after offsetting receipts and payments, they could apply to the Central Bank for purchase. After approval by the Central Bank, foreign exchange was sold at the statutory price, so as to appropriately limit the supply of foreign exchange. In June, regulations were successively issued to restrict the types of imported goods, and foreign exchange from exported goods should also be sold to national banks. On August 8, it was stipulated that applications for foreign exchange for goods shipped for import after January 1 of this year would no longer be accepted, except for necessities. The market's demand for foreign exchange could not be fully satisfied, and the so-called "black market" arose accordingly. The unofficial exchange rate of legal tender gradually declined from one shilling two and a half pence, reaching a low of seven pence eight seven five in August. However, since the second half of the year, the exchange rate in this black market has often hovered above eight pence. After the establishment of British and American loans, it became even more stable. It can be seen that the value of legal tender, even under the manipulation of the black market, can still maintain a considerable degree of stability.

Transfer Draft Discount: Shanghai's transfer drafts were originally scheduled to be cashed the next day. However, after the Ministry of Finance implemented the "Measures for Stabilizing Finance," the so-called interbank transfer drafts could only be used for transfers and could not be cashed, nor could they be used to purchase foreign exchange. Since its use was restricted, a discount method arose when it was exchanged for cash. This had already shown signs in the second half of last year, and this year it became even more intensified. Later, the Joint Reserve Board stepped in to maintain it and injected a large amount of funds, and it was then calmed down. By the end of this year, the amount of legal tender in the market had increased considerably, and the transfer draft discount had tended to decrease. Therefore, since the outbreak of the war, the Shanghai financial market has added a new type of fund. Customers often have to open two accounts, one for legal tender and one for transfer drafts, which is also an abnormal phenomenon of wartime finance. This year, the war gradually moved westward, and transportation between Shanghai and the interior became increasingly inconvenient. Before and during the war, the quantity of goods from Shanghai to the interior was quite large, while it was not easy to transport a large amount of local goods out of the interior and they were controlled by the government. The amount of funds remitted from the interior to Shanghai far exceeded the amount remitted from Shanghai to the interior, so the exchange rate became increasingly high, and there was the pain of not being able to adjust the exchange rate anywhere. In addition, the exchange rate between Shanghai and various ports in North China was also quite chaotic, so it was not easy for funds in various regions to support each other, which was also affected by the war.

Shanghai Capital: Since the war in the Nanjing and Shanghai areas, the number of people from the interior who came to Shanghai to seek refuge has increased day by day, and a large amount of capital from the war zone has flowed in. Moreover, a considerable amount of capital that purchased foreign exchange before and during the war has returned due to the accumulation of interest. Therefore, Shanghai's capital has gradually become abundant, and the current deposits of financial institutions have increased considerably. The market funds have become increasingly loose, and speculative activities have followed, from the buying and selling of foreign currencies, gold, and stocks to the hoarding of various commodities, which is even more prosperous than before the war. Using funds for unproductive purposes cannot but be regarded as a wartime economic worry.

Southwest Finance: After the government moved westward, the economic development of the Southwest cannot be delayed. In order to meet the needs of people in the interior, the major financial institutions in Shanghai have opened branches in important locations in various provinces in the Southwest, and the number has increased day by day. Many financial institutions in the war zone have also retreated to the Southwest with the government, and people's capital has gradually moved in to be used for local production enterprises. At present, Shanghai's capital lacks investment opportunities. If it can be transferred to the interior under safe principles, it will undoubtedly contribute to the economic development of the Southwest. All of the above are characteristics of wartime finance this year. Although it is not entirely satisfactory, if we understand the seriousness of this war and the vastness of its spread, we must regard the stability of the financial situation this year as a rare phenomenon. The government's efforts to protect the currency, ensure financial security, and maintain credit, as well as the cooperative assistance of friendly financial institutions, have all made great contributions.

(To be continued)
